/**
 * Decode an RLE-encoded array produced by the legacy rle1Decode format.
 * Elements that are plain numbers are emitted as-is.
 * Elements that are [count, value] arrays repeat the value count times.
 *
 * @param {Array} encoded - RLE encoded array
 * @returns {Uint8Array} Decoded bytes
 */
export const decodeRLE = (encoded) => {
  const output = [];
  for (const pair of encoded) {
    if (typeof pair === "number") {
      output.push(pair);
    } else {
      for (let i = 0; i < pair[0]; i++) output.push(pair[1]);
    }
  }
  return new Uint8Array(output);
};
 
/**
 * Pre-decoded boot disk image (8" SD, 256256 bytes).
 * Ready for use with createFloppy(BOOT_DISK, DISK_PROFILES["8SD"]).
 * @type {Uint8Array}
 */
export const BOOT_DISK = decodeRLE(BOOT_DISK_RLE);
